  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6e525fb8-6b2a-424e-b80e-fcdc63a51ff1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer3221308475577213562">From <i>USA Today, </i> bestselling author Jillian Dodd comes the first book in the addictive <i>Keatyn Chronicles</i> series. Discover a breathless fairy-tale romance with swoon-worthy characters, suspense, and a glittering celebrity world. Fans of <i>Gossip Girl, Pretty Little Liars</i>, and reality TV will devour this pulse-pounding, sexy teen drama set against the backdrop of Hollywood and</span>
  <span id="freeText3221308475577213562" style="display:none">From <i>USA Today, </i> bestselling author Jillian Dodd comes the first book in the addictive <i>Keatyn Chronicles</i> series. Discover a breathless fairy-tale romance with swoon-worthy characters, suspense, and a glittering celebrity world. Fans of <i>Gossip Girl, Pretty Little Liars</i>, and reality TV will devour this pulse-pounding, sexy teen drama set against the backdrop of Hollywood and an East Coast boarding school. <br /><br />Keatyn has everything she ever dreamed. Her life is following the script she wrote for the perfect high school experience. She’s popular, goes to the best parties, dates the hottest guy, and sits at the most-coveted lunch table. She’s just not sure she wants it anymore. Because, really, things aren’t all that perfect. Her best friend is threatening to tell everyone her perfect relationship is a scam. Her perfect boyfriend gets drunk at every party they go to. It’s exhausting always trying to look and act perfect. And, deep down, she isn’t sure if she has any true friends. <br /><br />To add to the drama, her movie star mom has a creepy stalker. A hot, older man flirts with her and tells her they should make a movie together. <br /><br />And she’s crushing on an adorable surfer. Dating him would mean committing social suicide<br /><br />So she writes a new script. One where all the pieces of her life will come together in perfect harmony. But little does she know, there's someone who will do anything to make sure that doesn’t happen.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3221308475577213562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_418855384" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/418855384" />
    <a title="M." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4898286-m"><img alt="M." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1330647592p2/4898286.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/418855384?book_show_action=true">Sep 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M." class="user" itemprop="url" name="M." href="/user/show/4898286-m">M.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">No one</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4898286-m?shelf=books-with-stupid-annoying-heroines">books-with-stupid-annoying-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4898286-m?shelf=books-i-hated">books-i-hated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4898286-m?shelf=ya-contemporary-romance">ya-contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer418855384" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11696299634895437298"><b>Worst.book ever. And here is why.<br/><br/>Review with Spoilers</b> <br/><br/>Let me just start by saying that I am so utterly pissed about this book. My reason to feel so has nothing to do with the fact that the main character wasn't very likeable. I mean, she is the daughter of Hollywood royalty, she is part of the popular girls, she is acts like a bitch then feels bad because she is acting like a bitch and want to change her ways, unfortunately is too weak to do so. I could deal with that. I could even deal with the</span>
  <span id="freeText11696299634895437298" style="display:none"><b>Worst.book ever. And here is why.<br /><br />Review with Spoilers</b> <br /><br />Let me just start by saying that I am so utterly pissed about this book. My reason to feel so has nothing to do with the fact that the main character wasn't very likeable. I mean, she is the daughter of Hollywood royalty, she is part of the popular girls, she is acts like a bitch then feels bad because she is acting like a bitch and want to change her ways, unfortunately is too weak to do so. I could deal with that. I could even deal with the fact that she couldn't make up her mind about which boy she wanted. She loves Brooklyn then she loses her virginity to Cush, then dreamy Cush acts out of character sending Keatyn back to Brookyln's arms again. But then Brooklyn starts to act like a dick and wants to change who Keatyn is, so Keatyn naturally breaks up with B and goes back to dreamy Cush. By then she realizes she actually loves Cush. That is when everything went down the drain and I was like are you freaking kidding me? What is this shit? <br /><br />You see, there was a stalker problem in this book (duh, obviously look at the title). But the stalker problem seemed to be more like a subplot because Keatyn's love woes took central stage throughout the whole book. So, 70 percent through the story, the stalker problem takes over. Instead of that being the climax of the plot where the stalker gets arrested, Keatyn finally starts to act like herself and have a HEA ending with Cush, the author decides to let the stalker go free. Yes people, a guy who attempted to kidnap a teenager goes free merely 20 minutes after such an attempt, even before the police got Keatyn's statement just because the stalker is gorgeous and has money? WTF? <i>(Okay, according to the author, the police did take Keatyn's statemente, however I don't recall reading about it. Such an important fact I shouldn't have to read between the lines or guess. It was not the first time that things weren't exactly clear in Jillian's books, so maybe she should take it into consideration next time)</i>. <br /><br />And then, to make things more freaking unbelievable, Keatyn gets sent to a boarding school in New York and is forbidden to tell Cush what happened to her because it could put him in danger ,however she is allowed to maintain contact with Brooklyn, how does that make sense? I hate when authors push their plot agenda without consideration to common sense. And how do you want me to believe that the teenager daughter of an A-list celebrity could go anywhere incognito? She didn't even change her unusual name, just her last name. Talk about lame. That was the biggest bullshit in Stalk me and it made me change a possible 3 star rating to 1.<br /><br />So yeah, I'm really angry that I wasted so much time reading Stalk me. This was me giving the benefit of the doubt. I liked That Boy but thought that That Wedding was weak. After Stalk me, I doubt that will be reading any more books by Jillian. Her writing style just doesn't do it for me.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11696299634895437298" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780985008666" href="/book/show/15841684-stalk-me">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer401072184" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16612684108711862339"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/33919c24-dd3a-41c8-8020-6e6b3fd1f640_zpsdaea6417.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750117.jpg' alt=' photo 33919c24-dd3a-41c8-8020-6e6b3fd1f640_zpsdaea6417.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Damn Disney, and all their happily-ever-after, unrealistic, bullshit stories.</blockquote>
</b><br/>Keatyn is not your average teenage girl, and this is not your average ya book. Keatyn is a sixteen year old girl who lives her life by the perfect script she has been writing for as long as she can remember. She is the daughter of a famous actress, America’s sweetheart, Abby Johnston. She lives in Malibu and has everything any other teen could possibly want. She is dating the most popular guy in high s</span>
  <span id="freeText16612684108711862339" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/33919c24-dd3a-41c8-8020-6e6b3fd1f640_zpsdaea6417.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750117.jpg" alt=" photo 33919c24-dd3a-41c8-8020-6e6b3fd1f640_zpsdaea6417.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Damn Disney, and all their happily-ever-after, unrealistic, bullshit stories.</blockquote>
</b><br>Keatyn is not your average teenage girl, and this is not your average ya book. Keatyn is a sixteen year old girl who lives her life by the perfect script she has been writing for as long as she can remember. She is the daughter of a famous actress, America’s sweetheart, Abby Johnston. She lives in Malibu and has everything any other teen could possibly want. She is dating the most popular guy in high school, friends with the most popular girls. She has it all... or does she? Keatyn sometimes feels like it’s all a lie. Her relationship, her popularity. She questions what it is she really wants. What type of person does she really want to be? Maybe it’s time to write a new script. One where all parts of her life can come together. It’s not as easy as it seems...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/ab150e5d-8b90-40ad-8047-f59f918e4ccc_zpsd3220e13.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750118.jpg" alt=" photo ab150e5d-8b90-40ad-8047-f59f918e4ccc_zpsd3220e13.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After ending her relationship Sander, her ‘perfect boyfriend’ and deciding to be just friends, Keatyn can go after who she really wants. Her best surfing pal and the guy she has been crushing on for FOREVER, Brooklyn. Brooklyn is chill, laid-back. He isn’t into the whole popularity thing. He is a few years older than Keats and he just wants to surf and hang. Keatyn has that side too. She loves to do those things. She wonders if she and B could possibly have a relationship. Now that she’s single, he seems to like her. Or does he just like hooking up with her? After ditching her for some surfing buddies, she starts hanging out with her good friend Cush... <br><br>Brandon Cushman. Cush has had it bad for Keatyn for a while, but she was always with Sander. Since Brooklyn ditched her, she gives Cush a try. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/f1e43895-9411-4a33-b100-051a39c9450f_zpsd9423a7a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750119.jpg" alt=" photo f1e43895-9411-4a33-b100-051a39c9450f_zpsd9423a7a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“I swear to God, I think my panties just melted off my body. How can Crush just talking sex make me hot?”</blockquote>
</i> It is impossible not to love Cush. He is so sweet, sexy, and he makes Keatyn feel like she is perfect just the way she is. All of her. <br>But does she really love Cush, or is he just a friend? When the mean girls from school interfere with their relationship, will it be able to survive?<br><br>Brooklyn gets back from his trip, and she realizes the whole thing was a misunderstanding. He didn’t ditch her to chill with other girls. Since Cush is out of the picture for the time being, she decided to chill with Brook for the summer...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/3dafb1a7-fcb1-417a-9166-048850ce877e_zps33b37169.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750120.jpg" alt=" photo 3dafb1a7-fcb1-417a-9166-048850ce877e_zps33b37169.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>"A thing of beauty is a thing of joy forever. It’s Keats. For my Keats.”</blockquote>
</i><br>Brooklyn is another boy you will love. He brings out the carefree, fun and laid-back version of Keatyn. He quotes her poetry, gets tattoo’s with her, surfs with her. She hangs with B and her buddy Damian (another guy you will love) most of the summer.She loves doing all the surfing and chilling with Brook, but he can’t really accept the part of her that loves to dance and go clubbing, who loves to shop and dress up. Can she be with someone who doesn’t want all of her? Only the side he likes?<br><br>Keatyn is back from the summer. On top of her complicated love life, there is some family drama. Her mom has a stalker. Someone who has been threatening her. And he has a new target. Keatyn. So Keats has to disappear for a while, to make herself safe. She is no longer Keatyn Douglas. Now, she is Keatyn Monroe. Keatyn has a plan for her new life at her new boarding school. A new script to follow... <br><b>
  <blockquote>I want people to like me, but I don't want to be popular. I'm going to make true friends. I'm not going to be a bitch or be fake, and I'm definitely not falling in love.</blockquote>
</b><br>But all that changes when she see’s him. The God of all Hotties...<br><b>
  <blockquote>This guy is almost too perfect looking to be real.</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/01c85fec-9258-48d0-9d3b-c606417157da_zps33e22706.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750121.jpg" alt=" photo 01c85fec-9258-48d0-9d3b-c606417157da_zps33e22706.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Keatyn meets many new faces at her new school. There are even more boys to add to the mix. A lot are cute, sweet, and fun. But no one catches her eye like Aiden. Too bad she isn’t going there. No relationship for her. Keatyn is kind of a hopeless romantic... You will have to see for yourself how long she sticks to that ;)<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/758ef38b-b2a0-45c5-8bca-d6ce0ea1fa81_zpsffa3afde.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750122.jpg" alt=" photo 758ef38b-b2a0-45c5-8bca-d6ce0ea1fa81_zpsffa3afde.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Stalk Me is one of those books that makes me want to be seventeen again... I want access to some of these hotties! Too bad I’m a decade too old for them. This book takes book boyfriends to a whole different level. I think I had at least 5 that I wanted in this book. Not only are the guys great, but you will fall in love with Keatyn. How many books have such a likable heroine? I want Keatyn to be my bff. Keatyn has a great heart, she is just a teenage girl trying to find herself. She’s not perfect, but she also isn’t a mean girl. She just wants to be her. Be real. Find people who like the real her. Thats not too much to ask, right?<br><br>Just when you think you’ve found your perfect guy, a new one comes a long and sweeps you off your feet! Here is a nice visual, so you can check out some of the hotties in Stalk Me:<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/d6b1c5c4-b164-4273-940c-526f74123ef3_zpsdd3419a8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389125i/750123.jpg" alt=" photo d6b1c5c4-b164-4273-940c-526f74123ef3_zpsdd3419a8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Stalk Me is fast paced, well written, unique, fun, and fabulous! Once you start reading, good luck putting it down! I fell in love with Jillian’s writing and characters when I read ‘This Boy’ and ‘This Wedding’, but I have to say I love this series even more! This is probably my favorite YA series. Lucky for you, the first four books are out now so you don’t have to wait to find out what happens next with Keatyn and her many boys! For those of you who haven’t read this fabulous series, what are you waiting for? The first book is currently free on Amazon and iTunes, pick it up and enjoy! <br><br>AMAZON LINK:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Stalk-me-Keatyn-Chronicles-ebook/dp/B0090SXRXK">http://www.amazon.com/Stalk-me-Keatyn...</a><br><br>ITUNES LINK:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/stalk-me./id555172123?mt=11">https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/stal...</a><br></span>

    <a title="♥ Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13161862-sarah"><img alt="♥ Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455167556p2/13161862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/524891644?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ Sarah" href="/user/show/13161862-sarah">♥ Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16038532-stalk-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13161862-sarah?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer524891644" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14481605514287508509"><i>Did I just read the same book as everyone else?</i><br/><br/>My rating for this book:<b> 1 STAR </b>(& only because I really liked Cush). <br/><br/>My main gripe with the story was Keatyn. She was wholly unlikable, and I could not relate to, or connect with her. I didn’t want to, either. She was a stuck-up, immature, spoiled ass brat that could not keep her hormones in check, and an attention seeking, flip-flopping, wishy-washy, people pleaser. <b>To state that she pissed me off, would be a huge understatement. </b><br/><br/>Her so-called “fr</span>
  <span id="freeText14481605514287508509" style="display:none"><i>Did I just read the same book as everyone else?</i><br /><br />My rating for this book:<b> 1 STAR </b>(&amp; only because I really liked Cush). <br /><br />My main gripe with the story was Keatyn. She was wholly unlikable, and I could not relate to, or connect with her. I didn’t want to, either. She was a stuck-up, immature, spoiled ass brat that could not keep her hormones in check, and an attention seeking, flip-flopping, wishy-washy, people pleaser. <b>To state that she pissed me off, would be a huge understatement. </b><br /><br />Her so-called “friends” were freaks. They consisted of back-stabbing, high-maintenance, insecure sluts, making characters from <i>Gossip Girl,</i> and <i>90212,</i> seem wholesome. <b>That’s just not cool. And that shit’s just not fun to read about, either. </b><br /><br />Oh, and the “romance” aspect of this story? HA! WHAT ROMANCE. I wanted to crawl under my blankets and hide. And I couldn’t help but wonder, <i>does this shit happen in real life?</i> Honestly, I’ve known a few promiscuous girls in high-school, but not really. <u> I’m very familiar with the Malibu scene;</u> unfortunately, not all “popular” girls are backstabbing sluts, nor are all surfers potheads, etc. <b>The whole story was overly dramatic, exaggerated, and unrealistic. And, the story just jumped all over the place; I couldn’t keep track of all of Keatyn’s hookups, and mind-changes. </b><br /><br />On that note, there were like, 5+ guys introduced in the story. WTH? Keatyn hooks up with multiple jerks, while going back and forth between multiple guys. <b>Keatyn doesn’t have any self-respect, or self-control. She was too desperate to lose her virginity, which made her look pathetic (IMO). </b>And, even before she loses it, she has commitment issues, and is perpetually confused about WHO SHE LIKES. The girl is annoying!<br /><br />And the whole “stalker” issue was SO LAME. Honestly, I’m probably a horrible person, but I WANTED something bad to happen to Keatyn, because her dumbass <i>almost</i> deserved it, with the way she was acting. Ugh. STUPID GIRL. <br /><br />I’m sorry. I just can’t stand <i>stupid</i> girls. And all the guys were ass-wipe, jerkoffs. Except Cush, until he got REPLACED – again &amp; again. <br /><br />AHHHHH! <br /><br />If you value your sanity, and want a more realistic, and actually romantic read, without all the unnecessary, dizzying, overly exaggerated, petty high-school drama on the “evils of popularity” and “hooking up with as many guys as you can,” shallow ass story-line, then<i> please,</i> <b> SKIP THIS ONE. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14481605514287508509" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_409491781" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/409491781" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/409491781?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer409491781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13076407814007280621"><a href='http://angiesdreamyreads.blogspot.com/2013/01/stalk-me-giveaway-and-review.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>THIS REVIEW HAS BEEN POSTED AT ANGIE'S DREAMY READS</a><br/><br/><b>4.5 CUSHTASTIC STARS</b><br/><br/>Stalk Me by Jillian Dodd was a fun filled, angsty ride. It's a mix between Gossip girl meets Beverly Hills 90210 and I loved it. Keatyn is the type of girl you always wanted to be in high school. She's the popular girl with a closet to die for and a never ending list of suitors after her. Jillian did an amazing job of writing some good teenage angst with a twist. I found myself devouring this book and fully invested in what K</span>
  <span id="freeText13076407814007280621" style="display:none"><a href="http://angiesdreamyreads.blogspot.com/2013/01/stalk-me-giveaway-and-review.html" rel="nofollow noopener">THIS REVIEW HAS BEEN POSTED AT ANGIE'S DREAMY READS</a><br /><br /><b>4.5 CUSHTASTIC STARS</b><br /><br />Stalk Me by Jillian Dodd was a fun filled, angsty ride. It's a mix between Gossip girl meets Beverly Hills 90210 and I loved it. Keatyn is the type of girl you always wanted to be in high school. She's the popular girl with a closet to die for and a never ending list of suitors after her. Jillian did an amazing job of writing some good teenage angst with a twist. I found myself devouring this book and fully invested in what Keatyn was going through.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Damn Disney, and all their happily-ever-after, unrealistic, bullshit stories." ~ Keatyn</i>
</b> <br /><br />Keatyn Douglas is not your average teenage girl, she is the daughter to a very famous mother named Abby Johnston and her stepfather is Hollywood icon Tommy Stevens. Growing up all she's wanted to do is be the popular girl, have the perfect boyfriend and have her life follow the perfect script (don't we all)!! But unfortunately life never follows the script we imagine and plan for ourselves and Keatyn's journey is pretty rocky. She has to deal with boyfriend drama, mean girls and fights to remain the person she is and not conform to her friends mean girl ways. On top of all that she faces a life threatening stalker issue that threatens her safety and leaves her life taking a new path.<br /><br />Stalk Me is overflowing with swoon worthy boys. It seemed every time I turned the page there was someone to drool over! Jillian did an incredible job with writing these characters. It started out with Sanders, your typical high school golden boy. He was sweet and amazing and came with a pretty big secret (which you'll discover as you read). We also meet Brooklyn who is your typical surfer boy, his laid back personality and smooth boy charms are extremely appealing. He know's how to woo a girl and his Keats for my Keats (poetry) were pretty damn incredible. Brooklyn is a little bit of a bad boy in this story, tending to lead Keatyn on. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"A thing of beauty is a joy forever." ~ Brooklyn. "You're single. I'm single. Let's mingle." ~ Cush </b>
</i><br /><br />Then we have Cushman!!! Oh girls (Mega swoon time). He had some amazing pick up lines!! Cush is the type of boy that you would have fell all over yourself for in high school. The boy you would have dreamt about at night and wanted to marry. The the type of boy that makes your heart skip a beat at the mere mention of his name! He's sweet and dreamy and caring but also is a little bit of a player which gives him this bad boy sex appeal. He has a major soft spot for Keatyn. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"You're single. I'm single. Let's mingle." ~ Cush</b>
</i> <br /><br />And last but certainly not least we have "The God of all Hotties," Aiden. This boy is so flipping gorgeous that he is called "The GOD of all hotties!" I mean come on, if for no other reason than that you need to read this book! Aiden was damn near delectable and I fell for him immediately leaving me torn between Team Aiden and Team Cush :/ It was that hard to choose. <br /><br />Overall I felt this book was really fantastic and I'm so excited there is going to be six books in this series. I love that we will be following Keatyn's life and will be able to see her mature and grow. I really loved Jillian's writing and felt it was a fun, faced paced, sexy and filled with an amazing amount of drama. Her story took off and left me not wanting to put my kindle down. I would highly recommend this series. It made it to my favorites shelf.<br /><br />♥ Angie </span>
  <a data-text-id="13076407814007280621" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/349870847?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews?shelf=september-2012">september-2012</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer349870847" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15872675516060066277"><b>Jillian Dodd still has my socks!</b><br/><br/>She knocked them off with <i>That Boy</i> & <i>That Wedding</i> and has decided not to give them back! I was a little worried before jumping in. I mean what if she comes down with a big case of suck!? It could happen!! It. Did. Not. Happen. Now Jillian Dodd has my socks and my knickers! <br/><br/>This book blew a fresh breath of different in all the right places. It was totally not what I expected! Speaking of...if you're expecting <i>Stalk Me</i> to be exactly like <i>That Boy</i> & <i>That Wedding</i> then</span>
  <span id="freeText15872675516060066277" style="display:none"><b>Jillian Dodd still has my socks!</b><br /><br />She knocked them off with <i>That Boy</i> &amp; <i>That Wedding</i> and has decided not to give them back! I was a little worried before jumping in. I mean what if she comes down with a big case of suck!? It could happen!! It. Did. Not. Happen. Now Jillian Dodd has my socks and my knickers! <br /><br />This book blew a fresh breath of different in all the right places. It was totally not what I expected! Speaking of...if you're expecting <i>Stalk Me</i> to be exactly like <i>That Boy</i> &amp; <i>That Wedding</i> then you <i>will</i> be disappointed. If you're expecting a unique YA-mature read with sharp edge and an addictive story line, then slap your own arse because this is the book for you! If it wasn't for the high school setting, I would have sworn this was new adult.<br /><br />Okay Keayton...I wanted to like her, I did, but I got distracted with wanting to punch her in the face. She stirred up a lot of emotions for me and whether the emotions were good or bad that is ALWAYS a positive thing. She's a 17 year old girl; she's gonna drive you crazy! She's having to learn lessons the hard way and it's extremely frustrating watching her do this! <br /><br />Finally...<br /><br /><b>TEAM CUSH!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br /><br />I liked Cush from the beginning, the VERY beginning. He gave me Cush-lash! Stalk Me? NO! Stalk you Cush! Cush! Cush! CUSH!!!! Cush-me? YES PLEASE! <br /><br />There's a scene between him a Keatyn that literally punched me right in the gut; I couldn't breath; I felt sick!! My emotions <i>had</i> emotions! I didn't understand why I was so invested, but I was...and I loved every second of it!!<br /><br />I still can't decide if I liked the ending or not. Other than breaking my heart, it was like the last few chapters were actually the first few chapters of the next book. A whole new story! Very interesting, very different. <br /><br />From the second I picked up <i>Stalk Me</i>, I could NOT put it down. It was unique, it was hot, it was sexy, it had Cush!!! You're heart won't be the only thing feeling, you'll feel it everywhere...EVERYWHERE!!!<br /><br />READ ON!!<br /><br /><br /></span>

Despite having privilege and wealthy Keatyn has always wanted a normal high school experience. She has been writing screen plays for how she thinks her high s</span>
  <span id="freeText1122367272952630408" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>I am now a Stalker</i> Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407613232i/10746603._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, its true Jillian Dodd has officially made me into a <i>stalker</i>. This is my third Dodd book and I absolutely adore her writing. <br><br>This is series is a little steamier, and still has a ton of heart. <br><br>Keatyn Douglas is the daughter of a <i>America’s Sweetheart</i> she grew up having the best of everything traveling the world. Despite having privilege and wealthy Keatyn has always wanted a normal high school experience. She has been writing screen plays for how she thinks her high school experience would play out, her first kiss, and even the first time she falls in love. <br><br>As you know people rarely get their Hollywood ending, and things don’t play out liked she planned.<br><br>This is the first book in the <i>Keatyn Chronicles</i> and it lays the foundation for the rest of the series. We meet Keatyn, her awesome family, horrible best friends, the many men who love Keatyn, and one who loves her too much. <br><br>I loved the journey Keatyn went through. It is something that most girls go through at some point in their life. It is hard to balance who are and who everyone wants you to be. It is hard to decide to be you when being popular and going with the flow is so much easier. I love how Keatyn was a good person with good intentions, and didn’t want to be a mean girl. <br><br>What did I love the most? <b>Cushman</b>, yes this little high schooler had me <b>
  <i>"lets mingle."</i>
</b> I loved him for Keatyn. <br><br>I couldn’t be more sold on this series, and I cannot wait to see what comes next for Keatyn and her friends. <br><br><br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><br><div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer348266762" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3438112507667567969">Spoiler Free Review<br/>4 STARS out of 5 STARS<br/>Genre: Mature-YA Romance<br/>Series: Book #1 in Keatyn Chronicles<br/><br/><i>Boy's Boy's Boy's Boy's<br/> Boy's I do adore.....</i>*sighs*<br/><b>Kiss me. Date me. Love me. Hate me.<i> STALK ME.</i> Yes this says it all.</b><br/><br/>Seems i found myself a new YA series to love <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13557124.Stalk_Me__The_Keatyn_Chronicles___1_' title='Stalk Me (The Keatyn Chronicles, #1) by Jillian Dodd' rel='nofollow noopener'>Stalk me.</a> left me wanting more and more. Thank goodness this is a six book series!!!!! YOU TOTALLY ROCK Jillian Dodd<br/><br/><b>Lights. Camera. Action.</b><br/>When she said Gossip Girl meets Hollywood she was not kidding this book brought 'The Life.' The </span>
  <span id="freeText3438112507667567969" style="display:none">Spoiler Free Review<br />4 STARS out of 5 STARS<br />Genre: Mature-YA Romance<br />Series: Book #1 in Keatyn Chronicles<br /><br /><i>Boy's Boy's Boy's Boy's<br /> Boy's I do adore.....</i>*sighs*<br /><b>Kiss me. Date me. Love me. Hate me.<i> STALK ME.</i> Yes this says it all.</b><br /><br />Seems i found myself a new YA series to love <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13557124.Stalk_Me__The_Keatyn_Chronicles___1_" title="Stalk Me (The Keatyn Chronicles, #1) by Jillian Dodd" rel="nofollow noopener">Stalk me.</a> left me wanting more and more. Thank goodness this is a six book series!!!!! YOU TOTALLY ROCK Jillian Dodd<br /><br /><b>Lights. Camera. Action.</b><br />When she said Gossip Girl meets Hollywood she was not kidding this book brought 'The Life.' The high life that is. Keatyn is living a life the average sixteen year old girl could only dream about. She gets to travel the world drive high end luxury/exotic cars, get into exclusive night clubs/parties and rub elbows with the rich and famous. Nice right? Yeah, I thought so too!<br /><br /><b>The Perfect Script</b><br />Keatyn Douglas is sixteen years old and is the daughter of Hollywood movie star Abby Johnston. She has a coveted wardrobe lives in Malibu and is dating a former child star. Sander. They make the perfect couple and everyone agrees. Keatyn is popular at school she is an 'It girl' and hangs with other 'It girls' her bestfriends Vanessa and RiAnne. <br /><b>Everything that glitters...</b> <br />Keatyn keeps up a facade that is something that becomes very clear. She is currently unhappy in her relationship and has been crushing on a surfer boy who lives down the street. Only problem is dating him is not even an option according to her bff's. <br />Yeah and what about them her so called bff's.... <br />Vanessa and RiAnne are mean girls on steroids. They are calculating and phoney it's obvious Keatyn does not really like them so much. She more so...puts up with them. <br />Oh, and then in addition to all that her movie star mom has a fan who has just been bumped up to <b>STALKER STATUS.</b> Yikes!<br /><br />Why you should read this book! <br />I cannot say much without giving too much away but i will say this. Keatyn's life revolves around<br /><b>-Sipping champagne at parties<br />- Shopping<br />- Hanging on tour with boy's<br />- Surfing with boy's<br />- Starting a Feud with girls<br />- Kissing boy's <br />- and dropping it like it's HOT <i>with boy's</i></b> <br />**Slowly grins**And i enjoyed every second! This chick has the fellas wrapped around her pinky all wanting a taste. And she gives them each a nibble, hmph and some a bite. Stalk Me has so many twists and an ending that leaves you salivating for more. Is that a good enough reason?!*smirks*<br /><br /><u>Thoughts</u><br />I loved the writing and the way Jillian Dodd incorporated a script as a theme throughout the book. That was a nice touch. I also like how she has Keatyn living this double life with the pressure to act a certain way. It made her more personable and I found it easy to relate to her on <i>that</i> level. I am very excited about this series and i cannot wait for book 2.<br /><u>The only thing i had a problem with...</u><br />Keatyn had way to much freedom i know that her lifestyle differs from the average. But... Her mom allowed her way to much freedom. <br /><br />My Rating<br />Characters- Lovable<br />Writing Style- Fun, Witty, and Savory<br />Plot/Storyline- Unputdownable,Fast paced with a touch of Suspense<br />Stean factor- Medium/Moderately Steamy<br />Overall- I loved it!!!!<br /><br /><b>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us all about it on Goodreads!</b><br /><br />To see more reviews go to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a> </span>

<div id="review_438909038" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/438909038" />
    <a title="Jenn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3957464-jenn"><img alt="Jenn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1360078699p2/3957464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/438909038?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenn" href="/user/show/3957464-jenn">Jenn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=hollywood">hollywood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=1-star-reads">1-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=annoying-protagonist">annoying-protagonist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=self-published">self-published</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer438909038" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17379278720840487314"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395050ra/760753.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I feel like I’ve lost a few brain cells. This book hurt to read. I was super excited to read this series. It’s no secret that I <b>LOVED</b> the <i>That Boy</i> series. But after reading this and looking back at <i>That Boy</i>, I think I was blinded by my pure love of Phillip and Danny that I just overlooked so many things. Unfortunately, for me, there were no likeable characters in <i>Stalk Me</i>, so there was nothing to hide behind. There will be spoilers in here, you have been warned. <br/><br/><i>Stalk Me</i> is the story of Keatyn, </span>
  <span id="freeText17379278720840487314" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395050ra/760753.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I feel like I’ve lost a few brain cells. This book hurt to read. I was super excited to read this series. It’s no secret that I <b>LOVED</b> the <i>That Boy</i> series. But after reading this and looking back at <i>That Boy</i>, I think I was blinded by my pure love of Phillip and Danny that I just overlooked so many things. Unfortunately, for me, there were no likeable characters in <i>Stalk Me</i>, so there was nothing to hide behind. There will be spoilers in here, you have been warned. <br><br><i>Stalk Me</i> is the story of Keatyn, daughter to a famous actress, whose life is ruled by money, glitz and glamour. It was like The Hills meets High School. Keatyn is 16, only wears designer clothes (which we are told in extreme detail every time), and only does things that keep her popular. She has to be the most self-centered, egotistical, idiotic child ever. Her inner monologue was like nails on a chalkboard. (Remember how I said it hurt to read this book?). It literally gave me a headache. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380379926ra/736464.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everything in her life revolved around status and looks. Great message to young girls out there, by the way. Keatyn would never do anything if she thought other people would look at her negatively – this included dating/breaking up with boys and having an actual opinion. She cared way too much about what other people thought that there was nothing original about her. <br><br>Now let’s talk about her love life *snort*. Did I mention every boy is in love with her? Oh, well they are. There’s the California surfer dude, there’s the stoned rich boy, there’s the older sophisticated gentleman…and that’s only in the beginning. While she’s a virgin in the beginning of the book, she loses it about halfway through and then becomes obsessed with sex. Apparently it’s the only way to solve arguments. And yes, she’s still 16. 16 and drinking in public places and going off to Europe alone with a boy. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/597068.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok, calming down…<br><br>Now, let’s talk about why the book is called Stalk Me. Keatyn’s mom has a stalker. So everyone in the house is put on high alert and told to avoid strangers and going places alone. Well, Keatyn (because she’s such a smart girl) decides that she doesn’t need protection and goes off on her own where she meets Vincent on the beach. Vincent is 30+ and immediately shows interest in our young Barbie. He’s a director and wants Keatyn to star in his movie. His movie -which is a remake of her mother’s first big role. Oh, and he also has a tattoo of her mother’s name on his arm.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395050ra/760754.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So what does Keatyn do? Why she goes out to dinner with him and continues to see him and chat about his movie of course. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/553062.gif" width="350" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When the stalker is finally revealed (three guess on who. Anyone?), plans immediately come together to get Keatyn out of Malibu. She needs to be safe. Witness Protection anyone? Not kidding, this was an actual suggestion. But Keatyn, not wanting to be hidden, comes up with her own plan:<br><br><i>“What if he thought I was a whore? What if I did a slutty video? Wouldn’t he hate me and stop being interested in me?”</i><br><br>Umm…what?<br><br>That gets dismissed and they decide to send our precious princess to a boarding school in Europe using a fake last name so no one knows who she is. After some tearful goodbyes to the two loves of her life (the surfer and the stoner), she’s heading to boarding school where upon arrival meets two new boys. <br><br>Shocking, I know. <br><br>The last handful of chapters are spent with Keatyn making out with two different boys in two days all the while telling people she has a boyfriend back home. But wait, it’s complicated. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395051ra/760755.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Disappointed doesn’t even begin to explain how I felt about this book. It was the most ridiculous storyline with asinine characters. Unbelievable situations with no emotional connections to anyone. And worst of all? Nothing was solved! While I have the next two in the series on my kindle, I do not know if I will continue it.<br><br>This review can also be seen <a href="http://www.bookjems.com/2013/05/book-review-stalk-me-keatyn-chronicles.html" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a> at my blog.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17379278720840487314" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer14260293985133468045"><b>Reread Review</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389295i/750340._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='460' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I want a redo of my high school experience with Keatyn Douglas as my best friend. Oh the clothes we would wear and oh the boys we would meet! <br/><br/>Keatyn is the daughter of a famous movie star and dreams of having a real high school experience. FYI her best friend is a gorgeous rock star!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I wanted to live out one big high school musical”.</i>
</b> <br/><br/>Keatyn has established herself as a popular girl, dating the popular boy all the while sitting at the popular table. Truth is she hates her girlfri</span>
  <span id="freeText14260293985133468045" style="display:none"><b>Reread Review</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389295i/750340._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="460" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I want a redo of my high school experience with Keatyn Douglas as my best friend. Oh the clothes we would wear and oh the boys we would meet! <br><br>Keatyn is the daughter of a famous movie star and dreams of having a real high school experience. FYI her best friend is a gorgeous rock star!<br><br><b>
  <i>“I wanted to live out one big high school musical”.</i>
</b> <br><br>Keatyn has established herself as a popular girl, dating the popular boy all the while sitting at the popular table. Truth is she hates her girlfriends and her boyfriend is kind of a dud. <br><br>Keatyn has had a crush on Brooklyn her surfer pal for the longest time. The problem is, Brooklyn only likes the surfer/laid back aspects of Keats. <b>
  <i>“A thing of beauty is a joy forever. It’s Keats. For my Keats.”</i>
</b> He hates her social life and fashion obsessions. Also, Brooklyn has professional surfing aspirations.<br><br>Then there is Cush….Cush goes to Keatyn’s school and definitely has a crush on her. He plays soccer and throws lots of parties. He is flirty and seems to follow her script:<br><br><i>
  <b>“When are you going to dump The Sandman? Come play with Cush?<br><br>“You’re single. I’m single. Let’s mingle." </b>
</i><br><br>They seem to be a perfect match… but danger in the form of a <b>STALKER</b> threatens Keatyn’s safety. She will have to abandon her family and friends to start anew. She enrolls in a private high school under a new last name and persona. <br><br>Keatyn more than embraces her new role and the opportunity to do things differently this time around. <br><br>This school has a plethora of hot guys in attendance. A shout out has to be made to “The God of All Hotties” Aiden Arrington and that delicious quarterback Dawson Johnson. I can’t wait to read more about these two!<br><br>So don’t change that channel because these important questions need to be answered: <br><br>Is Keatyn safe at her new school? <br><br>Will Cush and Keaytn meet again? <br><br>Where can I buy all those amazing outfits Keatyn wears?<br><br>Is Eastbrooke accepting late admissions?<br><br>Jillian Dodd sure has a winning series with The Keatyn Chronicles as there will be six books overall so get started today!<br></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351318041" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17033201907383343280"><b>Free on Amazon today 1/9 2014! Go grab it here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://ow.ly/soTjG'>http://ow.ly/soTjG</a></b><br/><br/><i>"The Keatyn Chronicles are similar to a television series. The books do not stand alone and the second books begins the same night book one ends."</i><br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623545.gif' width='390' height='250' alt='emmaswoon' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>There are too many delicious guys in this series. <b>Big swoon alert!</b><br/><br/><b>I love this series!</b> I only reread the last 20 percent because it is in the next book things get super good! <b>We have six books in this series, so this book sets the stage.</b> You have to read it, but unfortunately the first </span>
  <span id="freeText17033201907383343280" style="display:none"><b>Free on Amazon today 1/9 2014! Go grab it here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://ow.ly/soTjG">http://ow.ly/soTjG</a></b><br><br><i>"The Keatyn Chronicles are similar to a television series. The books do not stand alone and the second books begins the same night book one ends."</i><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/623545.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="emmaswoon" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>There are too many delicious guys in this series. <b>Big swoon alert!</b><br><br><b>I love this series!</b> I only reread the last 20 percent because it is in the next book things get super good! <b>We have six books in this series, so this book sets the stage.</b> You have to read it, but unfortunately the first 200 pages is exactly like Gossip Girl meets 90210.<br><br>I won't spoil it, but give book a chance! <b>If you are the least into YA/NA and you haven't read it - then you've been seriously missing out.</b> It is a happy book, with a tiny touch of angst. <b>It is like a colorful jar of candy!</b><br><br>Don't expect realism and enjoy all the delicious boys &lt;3. I really liked this one, but it is not a stand-alone novel so I'm kind of saving my five-stars to the next book which is one of my absolute favorites! <b>Me likey love a lot!</b><br><br>I would recommend reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11382346.That_Boy__That_Boy___1_" title="That Boy (That Boy, #1) by Jillian Dodd" rel="nofollow noopener">That Boy</a> so you know what an amazing author Jillian Dodd is! <b>She has a gift for creating yummy boys and a likable heroine. I am in awe! I might be one of her biggest fan. She is one of my absolute favorite authors.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17033201907383343280" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1268145313" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1268145313" />
    <a title="Muse-ic ♬" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36574090-muse-ic"><img alt="Muse-ic ♬" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1497741975p2/36574090.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1268145313?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Muse-ic ♬" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Muse-ic ♬" href="/user/show/36574090-muse-ic">Muse-ic ♬</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20836409-stalk-me">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=royalty-celebrities-or-rich-people">royalty-celebrities-or-rich-people</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=love-polygon">love-polygon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=insta-lust-love">insta-lust-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36574090-muse-ic?shelf=own-on-kindle">own-on-kindle</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1268145313" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14704650531146293892"><b>**spoilerzzzzzz*</b><br/><br/>2.5 <br/><br/>Is this a meaningful romance with cute relationships and cuteness to die for? Haha NOPE! The blurb got us there!<br/><br/>Is it like romances with 5+ boys involving the same shallow girl who cares more about the relationship than the boy involved? Yeeeeeeeeeeeees.<br/><br/>And you know what else? It made me want to pull my hair out multiple times. Meet Keatyn Douglas, stuck-up spoiled brat, daughter of a famous actress. Prepare yourselves for one of my longest reviews yet!<br/><br/>She drinks, does drugs,</span>
  <span id="freeText14704650531146293892" style="display:none"><b>**spoilerzzzzzz*</b><br><br>2.5 <br><br>Is this a meaningful romance with cute relationships and cuteness to die for? Haha NOPE! The blurb got us there!<br><br>Is it like romances with 5+ boys involving the same shallow girl who cares more about the relationship than the boy involved? Yeeeeeeeeeeeees.<br><br>And you know what else? It made me want to pull my hair out multiple times. Meet Keatyn Douglas, stuck-up spoiled brat, daughter of a famous actress. Prepare yourselves for one of my longest reviews yet!<br><br>She drinks, does drugs, and sleeps with her boyfriend, and her mother allows her to (notice how I wrote boyfriends with an "s"). Granted I guess it's better for her mom to know than to hide it from her mother, but you'd think there could be some regulation. This book glorifies these things, sending the message that if you drink alcohol, smoke weed or whatever, and have plenty of sex you will automatically be accepted into society's elite circle known as the "popular kids" in school. PUH-LEASE! As if we don't get enough of <i>that</i> in every advertisement or movie. I understand that many books have these things. They are totally normal in teen lives, but how are there no consequences to these things in this book? It's like a big advertisement! <i>Smoke weed and you'll be the most smokin' hot chick on the beach!</i><br>This book also makes it seem like all surfers smoke marijuana. Umm not true actually. And the "Romance" in this book? Utterly pitiful. Utterly. <br><br>Let's go through the romance sequence of this book.<br><br><b>Boyfriend #1:</b> Sander, an ex-child star who doesn't sleep with Keatyn because he wants to wait until marriage (though we find out later that he is actually gay). This pisses Keatyn off because they are supposedly considered the cutest/celebrity couple of the school. But God forbid, people cannot know that Keatyn and Sander haven't been sleeping together because her cool factor will automatically go down. <i>Oh no how preposterously disastrous!</i> They have a mutual break-up because Keatyn wants a boyfriend who will sleep with her and she is crushing on a surfer friend of hers. Also because Sander auditioned and was chosen for the part of Danny in a <i>Grease the Musical</i> remake. Moving on.<br><br><b>Boy-toy #2:</b> I said "boy-toy" and not "boyfriend" because the second boy Keatyn gets involved with is the surfer she crushed on, Brooklyn. She and Brooklyn had been friends for years and they liked each other (though for some reason they were convinced that they were in love) and during ONE night, they were in a hot tub together, kissed, then went upstairs to Brooklyn's room to confess their feelings and do some "stuff". Don't get too excited though. Keatyn is still a virgin after this. What bothers me is that they took to like third base after NEVER dating before. I get that they were friends, but not all "friends" can date and have the same relationship ever again. Sometimes it doesn't work. So after that night, Brooklyn leaves for somewhere and doesn't talk to Keatyn for three days (that's it). And when he does text her, he tells her they met some chill people, and this leads Keatyn to believe that Brooklyn's "chill" person or people was/were girls and that Brooklyn was sleeping with them. Why? I don't know. Keatyn is an idiot. So she wants to get back at him for breaking her heart. Moving on.<br><br><b>Boyfriend/toy #3:</b> Brandon Cushman, better known as "Cush". Cush is the soccer god of the school and a player. He doesn't date. Keatyn turns to him next because he always flirts with her and she decides he will give her what she wants (throwing away the flower of her virginity). So she talks to him and even though he never dated, it turns out it was because he was in love with her and wanted to date her. <i>How romantic!</i> Not really. Although I will say Cush may have been the most genuine character by far. So after dating for like two days (give or take), he takes her to a really nice hotel because everyone in Malibu is rich and can afford these things apparently, and they do the deed (Keatyn, of course, came prepared with sexy night clothes and lingerie). When Brooklyn came back, Keatyn acted all mushy with Cushy on the beach to get revenge for Brooklyn’s breaking her heart, which she actually did to herself. Oh wait! But that’s not all!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437370282ra/15579029.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A day before she went to France for something (I honestly have no clue what. I think her family had a house there), her ‘friend’ the social caste-obsessed Queen Bee Vanessa texts her and told her to come to a party at Cush’s house to say goodbye. It was a set-up. Turns out a girl named Mandy had drugged him with valium and was, ehrm….doing things….while Cush was drugged. She gave him so much he almost died. It was lucky that Keatyn showed up to save him and she didn’t blame him. But when Cush came to, he (for some reason I will never understand) blamed <i>Keatyn</i> for what happened and broke up with her. Cue Boy-toy/friend #4.<br><br><b>Boy-toy/friend #4:</b> Brooklyn. Again. They make up over the phone and she convinces him to come to France to see her where they can tour the coast and visit all the hotshot surf spots. While she is there alone. Aaaaand welcome teenage hormones! They’re <i>soooo</i> in <i>looove</i> and they act as if they are a newly married couple on their honeymoon. Oh the <i>roooomance</i>! However things start to fall apart when Keatyn tries to take Brooklyn dancing in techno clubs and whatnot, Brooklyn backs down and says he doesn’t like that stuff, or when she dresses up excessively, or puts on a lot of make-up. From here the relationship begins to spiral downward because it turns out that Brooklyn only really loves HALF of Keatyn, the surfer girl and chill part of her. She has to <i>beg</i> him to come to her big 17th birthday bash, which happens to be at a club back in Malibu. She also invites Cush to this despite the awkwardness because they are friends. Cush shows up having bought her an expensive pair of chic cowboy boots. She then discovers that Cush is “the boy who loves all of [her]”. They begin planning to get back together during her party after having broken up with Brooklyn. But wait. I thought she LOVED him. Yeah right. You don’t get over someone you’re in love with that fast News flash Keatyn! Buuuuuut everything goes to shit when someone tries and fails to kidnap her. Who is this mysterious kidnapper? Why, her mother’s creepy stalker who is none other than Vincent Sharpe (who actually has another name but I forgot it).<br> <br>And this whole time Vincent had been FLIRTING with her and she <i>flirted back!</i> With a thirty year old dude! I fail to see how <i>anything</i> could go wrong with <i>that</i>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438308462ra/15692240.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Basically he told her he handles the financial aspect of movies and he wants to do a remake of her mother’s old film, but with Keatyn as the lead instead of her mother because she is young and looks like her.<br>He stalked Keatyn’s mother for years as an obsessive fan, but he turned into a bad stalker and moved on to her blind daughter who didn’t suspect him until he tried TO KIDNAP HER! Where was I? Oh yeah! He turned into a bad stalker when Keatyn’s mother films graphic sex scenes and this made Vincent the Totally obvious Stalker hate her and accuse her of being a whore. You know what? The irony isn’t lost on me! Because as far as I’m concerned, what she acted was FAKE! What Keatyn was doing was REAL! You’d think Vincent would hate her too, because he actually knew about it! Whatever.<br><br>I don’t know if flirting with him counts Vincent as boy-toy #5 but we’ll give her the benefit of the doubt.<br>Vincent is caught but freed shortly after because there is no solid evidence against him. So they decide to change Keatyn’s last name to “Monroe” and give her a totally new and secret life in a far-away and very fancy boarding school. <i>There</i> she meets many new boys, though four of them stand out. Dallas and Riley are her friends, although she kisses and flirts back and forth with Riley. Aiden is the “God of all Hotties” to quote Keatyn. She kisses him and they start to have a thing. So what? That's boy-toy #5 or 6 right? The fourth one is Dawson, Riley’s older brother, who also happens to be hot. He just showed up in this one but I took a peek into the future and it looks like there may be a “thing” or more than a “thing” between them. We’ll call him boy-toy #5.5 or 6.5, depending on if you count Vincent or not. I do. Also when they didn’t know who the stalker was, and they were getting the strange notes, did it ever occur to them to check for fingerprints? Duuhh!<br><br>Wow look at all those boys in one book! Now she may be a “men’s lady”, but many instances lead us to confirm that all she really wants is sex. She starts off the book as a virgin, but constantly <i>whines</i> about about it because, God forbid, she can’t be in the popular crowd <i>and</i> be a virgin. It’s much too uncool! She was also very desperate for people to find out that she was having sex.<br><br><br>Also Keatyn describes her clothes a lot, which isn’t necessarily a bad thing. Description is good. It’s bad when you use the same word over and over again, like the word “cute” in this case. Her shoes are “cute” a lot. <br><br>Let’s talk about the ending for a second. Worst. Ending. Ever. And it wasn’t a cliffhanger. It <i>should</i> have been. It should have been something like “And so I went off to boarding school” (except more eloquently). Oh no. The ending was AFTER she got to boarding school and met guys and made sports teams. It was too happy and too anticlimactic. Seriously if the author wants people to be hooked enough to read the next book, there should be more than one unanswered question. It was lame and equivalent to a statement like “and they stared at the sky” in excitement.<br><br>The only reason I'm continuing is because I'm hoping Vincent catches up with her *Evil laugh*.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422793285ra/13545812.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14704650531146293892" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_640939072" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/640939072" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/640939072?book_show_action=true">Mar 01, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

          marked it as did-not-finish




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer640939072" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14986214859637571281"><b>DNF with 7 hours and 58 mins left</b><br/><br/>I did the audio version of this book and I know I didn't really give it a shot, but I TRIED I REALLY DID.<br/><br/>First off, I met Jillian Dodd at a book signing once and she is the NICEST person ever. So it pains me to say this and in the end this book is probably not geared towards me.<br/><br/><b>I love a good ditzy, glamorous and beautiful Heroine, but I could for the life of me not connect with her.</b> Let me just say this, I HATED the narrator. She spoke too fast and when I tried t</span>
  <span id="freeText14986214859637571281" style="display:none"><b>DNF with 7 hours and 58 mins left</b><br /><br />I did the audio version of this book and I know I didn't really give it a shot, but I TRIED I REALLY DID.<br /><br />First off, I met Jillian Dodd at a book signing once and she is the NICEST person ever. So it pains me to say this and in the end this book is probably not geared towards me.<br /><br /><b>I love a good ditzy, glamorous and beautiful Heroine, but I could for the life of me not connect with her.</b> Let me just say this, I HATED the narrator. She spoke too fast and when I tried to slow it down, it sounded awkward. I felt like she read the book really choppy and her voice sounded like she had something stuck up her noise. She did however sound young and it fit the youthful personality of the character.<br /><br />I picked up this book because of the glowing reviews, but in the end it wasn't for me. I couldn't understand her position towards guys. She had a boyfriend, then she had a crush on someone, she wanted her boyfriend to have sex with her, but then she would play out these scenes? It was just hard to follow and I need easy books when I listen to audio. <br /><br />Also, the name dropping of fashion was making my head hurt. I'm a fashion girl. I love purses, high-end brands, etc, but it just felt like it was over kill in the book. I get it, she likes expensive stuff.<br /><br />Maybe I need to read this book instead of listening to it. I just had to stop with the audio, I was getting really angry as each minute I was listening. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14986214859637571281" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

To have to best high school experience- being popular, dating the hottest guy, having great friends. Unfortunately for Keatyn, things are never as perfect as they look on the outside. Keatyn struggles with trying maintain the a perfect persona, while trying to figure out who she is. Let's not forget the psychotic stalker who threatens her safety and alters the course of her life. Keatyn's life is definitely not following her script, but maybe she will find true happiness through the madness.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/QEoLiGV" rel="nofollow noopener">

And Keatyn's feelings for these guys are all over the place, she had my head spinning. I loved <i>"You're single. I'm single. Let's mingle." -Cush</i>.<br><br>I really enjoyed this story, it kept me entertained and I look forward to continuing Keatyn's story.<br><br><a href="http://s293.photobucket.com/user/sleepie816/media/BeFunky_wave2jpg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_440515209" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/440515209" />
    <a title="Tammy  Zautner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6539323-tammy-zautner"><img alt="Tammy  Zautner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1461189789p2/6539323.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/440515209?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tammy  Zautner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tammy  Zautner" href="/user/show/6539323-tammy-zautner">Tammy  Zautner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer440515209" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2926278051342413845">I think I am in the minority here. <br/><br/>What did I like about this book? Cush! Loved him. The End. <br/><br/>What did I not like about this book? <br/><br/>Well for starters, this is a story about a high school girl; I am I betting its reader base will be other high school girls. Therefore, let us glamorize the use of sex, drugs, and bullying. Keaton is a 16-year-old girl who has multiple bed partners within days of each other. The one too many boys (at least 4 or 5) involved made our girl look slutty. If that was not e</span>
  <span id="freeText2926278051342413845" style="display:none">I think I am in the minority here. <br /><br />What did I like about this book? Cush! Loved him. The End. <br /><br />What did I not like about this book? <br /><br />Well for starters, this is a story about a high school girl; I am I betting its reader base will be other high school girls. Therefore, let us glamorize the use of sex, drugs, and bullying. Keaton is a 16-year-old girl who has multiple bed partners within days of each other. The one too many boys (at least 4 or 5) involved made our girl look slutty. If that was not enough, the drugs and drinking on every other page along with the fact that her mother was OK with it all (yes her mother knew all about it) majorly pissed me off! I swear if I had to read any more about this teenager’s adventure with drinking excessively/getting high and having insane amounts of sex fantasies/cravings I was going to lose my ever-loving mind. I am no prude, but seriously?! <br /><br />I really wanted to like this book and root for my favorite in the love triangle, but I totally did not understand the whole ending. I was left shaking my head and rereading to see if I missed anything.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2926278051342413845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
